The BMW M5 is a high-performance variant of the BMW 5 Series marketed under the BMW Msub-brand. It is considered an iconic vehicle in the sports sedan category. The M5 has always been produced in the sedan (saloon) body style, but in some countries the M5 has also been available as a wagon (estate) from 1992 to 1995, from 2006 to 2010, and since 2024. The first M5 model was hand-built in 1985 on the E28 535i chassis with a modified engine from the M1 that made it the fastest production sedan at the time. M5 models have been produced for every generation of the 5 Series since 1985.

This swimming pool was built on top of the Market Square Tower apartment complex and is called the tallest pool in Texas. It stretches 10 feet (3 meters) out from the building, with a section made of 8-inch (20 cm) thick plexiglass, so swimmers can see the city 500 feet (150 meters) below. It is held up by two concrete cantilevers, one on each side. The tower and pool were finished in November 2016 and were designed by Jackson and Ryan Architects. When a sommelier rotates a wine glass, the rotational forces help keep the wine inside the glass due to a combination of centrifugal force and the shape of the glass. the rotational motion helps to stabilize the wine within the glass due to centrifugal force, the inward curve of the glass, smoother fluid dynamics, and surface tension. This combination of factors makes it less likely for the wine to spill out when the glass is rotated properly. Maharashtra has recorded 91 cases of the new FLiRT COVID-19 variants, which also accounts for more than a third of cases in the US. However, there is no cause for worry as of now, a top expert said on Sunday. The new set of variants dubbed FLiRT, majorly includes KP.1.1, and KP.2 strains. These are named based on the technical names for their mutations, one of which includes the letters "F" and "L", and another of which includes the letters "R" and "T". Genome sequencing of March and April showed that Maharashtra has 91 cases of KP.2 â€” Pune (51), Thane (20), Amravati (7) Aurangabad (7), Solapur (2), Ahmednagar (1), Nashik (1), Latur (1), and Sangli (1). "What we see now, is the result of genome sequencing of the last two months, that is March and April. So, there is no cause of concern immediately as out of the 91 cases, not a single death, hospitalisation, or severe disease has been reported," infectious disease expert Dr Ishwar Gilada, told IANS. "Even the test positivity rate is around 1%," he added. Dr Rajesh Karyakarte, Maharashtraâ€™s genome sequencing coordinator, said that KP.2 has become the predominant COVID-19 strain in the state. However, there hasnâ€™t been a corresponding increase in hospitalisations or severe cases, The Times of India reported. FLiRT variants come from the lineage of the highly transmissible and immune system-evading Omicron. First identified globally in January, KP.2 is a descendant of Omicronâ€™s JN.1. According to the data from the US Centers for Disease Control and Prevention, KP.2 accounted for about one in four or 25% of new sequenced cases in the country in the last weeks of April. Similar to previous variants, the symptoms typically include a sore throat, runny nose, congestion, tiredness, fever (with or without chills), headache, muscle pain, and sometimes loss of taste or smell. . . . #TheTatva #TtavaNdews #India #Maharashtra #COronavirus #COVID19 #Pandemic #ENdemic #Vaccine #Flirt #Spread #Virus #US #Aurangabad #Nashik #Pune #Thane #Mumbai #Record

Listen! Here's some interesting facts about the exam NEET :- NEET is a national-level entrance examination conducted by the National Testing Agency (NTA) for admission to undergraduate medical and dental courses in government and private medical colleges in India. NEET was introduced in 2013 to streamline the medical entrance exams and reduce the burden on students appearing for multiple exams conducted by different states and institutions. The exam pattern of NEET includes multiple-choice questions (MCQs) from subjects like Physics, Chemistry, and Biology (Botany and Zoology). It also has a negative marking scheme for incorrect answers. NEET replaced the All India Pre-Medical Test (AIPMT) and all other individual state-level medical entrance exams to ensure a standardized process for medical admissions across the country. NEET is considered one of the toughest entrance exams in India due to the high level of competition and the vast syllabus that students need to cover. DID YOU KNOW THIS BEFORE?

Oo dear loveâ¤ï¸ In the quiet moments of dawn, When the world is soft and still, I see your beauty, my love, In ways that time can't steal. Your eyes, deep like the night sky, Hold secrets and dreams untold. Long lashes like whispers of the wind, Brush gently, tender and bold. Your messy hair, a wild embrace, Each strand a tale of grace. Apply to it and pass through!! . #year #time #memory #ageing #age #pain #forget #researchgoesslowly #postdoc #postdoclife #PhD #PhDlife #masterstudent #PhDstudent #phdstudentlife #student #researcher #college #researcherlife
